[[Jonny]]

Use [[Tragic Hero]] with any [[Village]] or [[+2 Action]] card that lets you trash multiple and gain a lot of [[Gold]]. Useful to also have a card like [[Importer]] that lets you gain a [[Costs 5]] card. Then you end up [[Causes Many Cards|with many cards]] and many buys

Also good with [[Market Towns]] or anthing that gets you [[Villager]]s so that you can keep cycling until you get it.



[[Game Log]]:

---

```html
        <!---->
    </log-line>
    <!---->
    <log-line ng-repeat="l in logController.entries" log-entry="l" show-undos="logController.shouldShowUndos()" class="">
        <!---->
        <!---->
    </log-line>
    <!---->
    <log-line ng-repeat="l in logController.entries" log-entry="l" show-undos="logController.shouldShowUndos()" class="" style="">
        <!---->
        <div class="log-line " style="padding-left: 0%; width:98%;" ng-repeat="line in $ctrl.lines">
            <!---->
            <div class="log-line-block" ng-repeat="block in line"><span ng-style="{}" on-long-press="$ctrl.study(block)" ng-right-click="$ctrl.study(block)"></span></div>
            <!---->
            <div class="log-line-block" ng-repeat="block in line"><span ng-style="{&quot;color&quot;:&quot;rgb(255, 0, 0)&quot;}" on-long-press="$ctrl.study(block)" ng-right-click="$ctrl.study(block)" style="color: rgb(255, 0, 0);">A</span></div>
            <!---->
            <div class="log-line-block" ng-repeat="block in line"><span ng-style="{}" on-long-press="$ctrl.study(block)" ng-right-click="$ctrl.study(block)"> buys and gains </span></div>
            <!---->
            <div class="log-line-block" ng-repeat="block in line"><span ng-style="{&quot;color&quot;:&quot;#66CD00&quot;,&quot;cursor&quot;:&quot;help&quot;}" on-long-press="$ctrl.study(block)" ng-right-click="$ctrl.study(block)" style="color: rgb(102, 205, 0); cursor: help;">an Estate.</span></div>
            <!---->
        </div>
        <!---->
        <!---->
    </log-line>
    <!---->
    <log-line ng-repeat="l in logController.entries" log-entry="l" show-undos="logController.shouldShowUndos()" class="">
        <!---->
        <!---->
    </log-line>
    <!---->
    <log-line ng-repeat="l in logController.entries" log-entry="l" show-undos="logController.shouldShowUndos()" class="">
        <!---->
        <div class="log-line " style="padding-left: 0%; width:98%;" ng-repeat="line in $ctrl.lines">
            <!---->
            <div class="log-line-block" ng-repeat="block in line"><span ng-style="{}" on-long-press="$ctrl.study(block)" ng-right-click="$ctrl.study(block)"></span></div>
            <!---->
            <div class="log-line-block" ng-repeat="block in line"><span ng-style="{&quot;color&quot;:&quot;rgb(255, 0, 0)&quot;}" on-long-press="$ctrl.study(block)" ng-right-click="$ctrl.study(block)" style="color: rgb(255, 0, 0);">A</span></div>
            <!---->

            <!---->

</div>
```
